3788 // BAND 5: High-Shelf filter
3789 else if(Display.currentBand == 5) {
3790 EQ_BAND5.cutoff = Display.Filter_Cutoff[Display.currentBand-1];
3791 SetupHighShelf(&EQ_BAND5, EQ_BAND5.cutoff, EQ_BAND5.Q, EQ_BAND5.dBGain);
3792 }
3793 break;
3794 case 3:
3795 // Gain
3796
3797 /*****************************
3798 * @brief HS / LS / PEQ Gain: -18dB to 6dB
3799 * @brief Scaling 4095 (ADC_value) to a range of 24dB by dividing with 170.625
3800 * @brief Center around 0dB by subtracting (4095/(2*170.625))
3801 * @brief Subtract 6dB for final adjust
3802 ******************************/
3803 Display.Filter_Gain[Display.currentBand-1] = ((float)Display.ADC2inputs[2] / 170.625)-(4095/(2*170.625))-6;
3804
3805 // BAND 1: Low-Shelf filter
3806 if(Display.currentBand == 1) {
3807 EQ_BAND1.dBGain = Display.Filter_Gain[Display.currentBand-1];
3808 SetupLowShelf(&EQ_BAND1, EQ_BAND1.cutoff, EQ_BAND1.Q, EQ_BAND1.dBGain);
3809 }
3810 // BAND 2: Peaking-EQ
3811 else if(Display.currentBand == 2) {
3812 EQ_BAND2.dBGain = Display.Filter_Gain[Display.currentBand-1];
3813 SetupPeakingEQ(&EQ_BAND2, EQ_BAND2.cutoff, EQ_BAND2.Q, EQ_BAND2.dBGain);
3814 }
3815 // BAND 3: Peaking-EQ
3816 else if(Display.currentBand == 3) {
3817 EQ_BAND3.dBGain = Display.Filter_Gain[Display.currentBand-1];
3818 SetupPeakingEQ(&EQ_BAND3, EQ_BAND3.cutoff, EQ_BAND3.Q, EQ_BAND3.dBGain);
3819 }
3820 // BAND 4: Peaking-EQ
3821 else if(Display.currentBand == 4) {
3822 EQ_BAND4.dBGain = Display.Filter_Gain[Display.currentBand-1];
3823 SetupPeakingEQ(&EQ_BAND4, EQ_BAND4.cutoff, EQ_BAND4.Q, EQ_BAND4.dBGain);
3824 }
3825 // BAND 5: High-Shelf filter
3826 else if(Display.currentBand == 5) {
3827 EQ_BAND5.dBGain = Display.Filter_Gain[Display.currentBand-1];
3828 SetupHighShelf(&EQ_BAND5, EQ_BAND5.cutoff, EQ_BAND5.Q, EQ_BAND5.dBGain);
3829 }
3830 break;
3831 case 4:
3832 // Q-Factor Source
3833 break;
3834 case 5:
3835 // Cutoff Source
3836 break;
3837 case 6:
3838 // Gain Source
3839 break;
3840 default:
3841 break;
3842 }
3843 }

3846 Paint_DrawFilledRectangle(&paint, Display.value_start_x_position-30, CASE2, Display.value_end_x_position, CASE2+VALUE_ROW_LENGTH, UNCOLORED);
